***индус.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:индус.html>инду́с</a> (17032)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:индус.html>инду́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">indús</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:индус.html>инду́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:индус.html>инду́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:индус.html>инду́сов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">инду́ска</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Hindu (<i>male</i>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Indian (<i>a man from India</i>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Hindu</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">индуи́ст</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">induíst</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Indian</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:индиец.html>инди́ец</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">indíjec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***индустриальный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:индустриальный.html>индустриа́льный</a> (8212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:индустриальный.html>индустриа́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">industriálʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>industrial <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relating to industry</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:индустриальный.html>индустриа́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:район.html>райо́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>industriálʹnyj</b> rajón</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>industrial</b> district</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***иней.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́ней</a> (9246)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьnьjь</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьnьje</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьnьja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hoar-frost, rime</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*H₁eyH-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́ней</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ínej</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́нея</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́неи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́неев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hoarfrost, frost, rime
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>190-</b> [1886],  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>),  “Шуточка”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>Повести</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассказ.html>расска́зы</a></cite>  | <cite>Stories and tales</cite> |  (<a href = vnd.unilang:сочинение.html>Сочине́ние</a> |  2), Saint Petersburg |  A.F. Marx |  translated as  “A Little Game”, in Katherine Tiernan O'Connor, transl., <cite>Anton Chekhov's Selected Stories</cite>, W.W. Norton, 2014, page 57:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ясный.html>я́сный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:зимний.html>зи́мний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полдень.html>по́лдень</a>... <a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́з</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крепкий.html>кре́пок</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:трещать.html>трещи́т</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> на́деньки, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>де́ржит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:покрываться.html>покрыва́ются</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:серебристый.html>серебри́стым</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́неем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кудри.html>ку́дри</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:висок.html>виска́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушо́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:верхний.html>ве́рхней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губо́й</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jásnyj, zímnij póldenʹ... Moróz krépok, treščít, i u Nádenʹki, kotóraja déržit menjá pod rúku, pokryvájutsja serebrístym <b>ínejem</b> kúdri na viskáx i pušók nad vérxnej gubój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A clear winter noonday... The frost is hard, it crackles, and Nadenka, who is holding me by the arm, has a silvery <b>glaze</b> coating the curls on her temples and the down on her upper lip.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́нея</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bélyj ot <b>íneja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">white with <b>frost</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> white hair</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инерция.html>ине́рция</a> (8331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инерция.html>ине́рция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inɛ́rcija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инерция.html>ине́рции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инерция.html>ине́рции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инерция.html>ине́рций</a></b>)
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">incassare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to collect cash, put in a box</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инкассатор.html>инкасса́тор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inkassátor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инкассатор.html>инкасса́тора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инкассатор.html>инкасса́торы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инкассатор.html>инкасса́торов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>money collector, collection agent, cash messenger</li></ol>

***инквизиция.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инквизиция.html>инквизи́ция</a> (9894)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инквизиция.html>инквизи́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inkvizícija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инквизиция.html>инквизи́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инквизиция.html>инквизи́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инквизиция.html>инквизи́ций</a></b>)
</p>

***инкрустировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инкрустировать.html>инкрусти́ровать</a> (28681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">inkrustieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">incruster</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:инкрустировать.html>инкрусти́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inkrustírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to incrust, to inlay</li></ol>

***иногда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иногда.html>иногда́</a> (337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">inój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-гда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-gda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kogdá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for the origin of the last element.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иногда.html>иногда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inogdá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sometimes, at times</li>
<li>now and then</li></ol>
